Important News 2

The Jiaoji Railway After the Great War 59

Jinan Dispatch: The Jiaoji Railway, since its construction and opening to traffic by the Germans, has suffered war damage for the first time this year. The railway's Chairman, Sa Fujun, and Deputy Director of Transportation, Tan Shukui, arrived in Jinan this morning (the 10th) on a special train with Finance Minister Song Ziwen. Upon arrival, Mr. Ping asked Tan about the purpose of their visit. Tan replied that the Chairman's visit to Jinan was to accompany Minister Song to attend Chairman Han's inauguration ceremony and to inspect the railway's war losses. Ping then inquired about the extent of the war losses, to which Tan provided the following information:

(1) Losses of Business and Property: The railway's usual monthly revenue is around one million yuan. This year, due to the suspension of operations for forty-five days because of the war, the loss is about 1.5 million yuan. Although traffic resumed during the four months before and after the war, the reduction in business resulted in another loss of approximately 1.5 million yuan. Ten bridge sections were bombed, including the largest, the Zihe Bridge, resulting in a loss of over one million yuan. Additionally, the reduced income during the suspension of operations, coupled with the requirement to pay workers three days' wages for each day worked in the war zone, resulted in considerable expenses. The total estimated loss is around 4.5 million yuan.

(2) Losses of Various Vehicles: The railway originally had 105 locomotives, 219 passenger cars, 1,679 freight cars, and 14 miscellaneous cars. During the retreat of the Jin Army, they took with them 3 locomotives and 54 passenger and freight cars. Furthermore, when the National Army recovered Jinan and transported troops south, they requisitioned another 5 trains, totaling 5 locomotives and over 100 freight cars. Recently, 2 more trains were transferred, including 2 locomotives and over 30 passenger and freight cars. In total, approximately 7 locomotives and 200 passenger and freight cars were transferred. Last year, Yang Hucheng's army took 7 locomotives and over 100 freight cars south, and Sun Dianying's army took 2 locomotives and 50 freight cars, which are not included in the above figures (the locomotives taken by Yang and Sun belonged to the Jiaoji Railway, but most of the remaining cars belonged to other railways). Currently, the First Army Corps is still occupying over 200 cars on the railway. Although the cars are still on the railway, they are not under the control of the railway bureau, which still affects business.

(3) Current Business Revenue and Expenses: Since the resumption of traffic on the 20th of last month, the average daily revenue until the end of the month was 15,000 yuan. This month, up to today (the 10th), the average daily revenue is 25,000 yuan, amounting to just over 700,000 yuan per month. However, monthly expenses, including employee salaries and all other expenses and materials, amount to 700,000 yuan, and monthly interest payments on Japanese debt amount to 200,000 yuan, resulting in a significant deficit. Interest payments on Japanese debt in the second half of the year will be particularly difficult. Currently, 80% of freight cars have been restored, with eight freight trains running daily between Qingdao and Jinan (four from each direction). Branch lines, which originally had sixteen freight trains running daily (eight in each direction), are now only running six. Passenger traffic has been restored to 80%, with four passenger trains running between Qingdao and Jinan, and two between Jinan and Fangzi. However, the special express night trains No. 1 and 2 have not yet been restored due to the incomplete suppression of bandits along the route.

(4) Future Rectification Methods: The railway has never experienced war before, and this is the first time. The order of the entire railway has deteriorated significantly, and the morale of the employees has also been greatly affected. Forty to sixty troop trains used to run daily between Qingdao and Zihedian, one can imagine the utter devastation. Rectification is no easy task. Due to the shortage of freight cars, it has been decided to increase the turnover rate and run more trips. An order has been placed with Belgium for 100 new freight cars, each with a load capacity of 40 tons, which is equivalent to about 260 of the railway's current freight cars (the current Jiaoji Railway freight cars each have a load capacity of only 15 tons). These new cars are expected to cost 800,000 yuan, and a batch is expected to arrive in October. Approval has also been obtained from the Ministry of Railways to order six new boilers, which will slightly alleviate the freight situation. As for the bridges, the required funds are too large, and repairs cannot be made until next year. The Transportation Department has scheduled a section meeting in Jinan this Saturday, with the heads of each transportation section and the department's section chiefs attending to discuss railway rectification matters. (September 10th)

Closing of the Huai River Planning Conference 60

The Huai River Commission convened a planning discussion conference on the Huai River beginning on the 11th of this month. On the 12th, the conference continued, still chaired by Chief Engineer Li. From 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM, all major water conservancy issues related to the guiding of the Huai River were discussed and resolved. The items resolved that day included: (1) Issues regarding the management of the middle and upper reaches of the Huai River; (2) Issues regarding the navigation and irrigation of the Huai River; (3) Issues regarding the management of the Yi, Si, and Shu Rivers; (4) The relationship between the Huai and Yellow Rivers. In addition, Mao Yisheng and others, representatives from the Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Commission, proposed the printing and distribution of the Huai River conference's technical report and the opinions of the representatives, seeking opinions and organizing the Huai River Commission's evaluation council and the reconstruction of the Sanjiangying active barrage. Also, Pei Yixiang, the representative from Anhui Province, proposed that the Huai River's middle reaches' levee engineering project be included in the first phase of the construction plan. Li Shutian, a member, proposed that the Construction Committee collect survey data, deliberate on a unified plan, and jointly implement it with various water conservancy agencies. All these proposals were approved on the spot. Finally, it was resolved to publicly recommend Member Shen Baixian to draft a report. After the Huai River Commission completed its discussions, photos were taken and the meeting adjourned happily. It is reported that representatives who came from afar from Peiping, Tianjin, Zhenjiang, and Shanghai, such as Wang Jixu, Li Shutian, Shen Baojun, Pei Yixiang, and Mao Yisheng, all departed for their respective destinations that evening due to their other duties.

Finance and Education in Jiangxi 61

Political Expenses in Arrears for Several Months

Primary and Secondary Schools Completely Suspended

Nanchang Dispatch: Jiangxi's annual budget for both revenue and expenditure is 14 million yuan, with an average monthly revenue and expenditure of one million yuan. However, since last year, the bandits and communists have devastated the local economy. Gannnan and Ganxi have no revenue at all, and only the ten or so counties near the provincial capital in Gandong and Ganbei have a small amount of funds to contribute. Monthly revenue is about 100,000 yuan (about one-tenth of the budget), which is tens of thousands of yuan short. The provincial government believes that suppressing the bandits is the only way out at present, so it has decided to concentrate financial resources solely on suppressing the bandits. In terms of political expenses, only the most urgent matters are addressed, resulting in accumulated arrears of several million yuan. Some agencies have received salaries up to June, some up to May, and some even only up to March or April. Public officials are complaining incessantly. In order to increase the province's revenue, the Finance Department issued a proclamation to auction off the city moat land in the provincial capital, estimating that it could generate more than one million yuan. However, in these times of popular poverty and financial exhaustion, no one has inquired about it. More than one million yuan worth of rice export permits (each permit taxing two yuan per picul of exported rice) have been printed and requests for them are pouring in, but it is only a drop in the bucket. Finance Director Chen went to Xunyang in the past month to personally borrow more than 200,000 yuan from the refined salt merchants for the expenses of suppressing the bandits, but it was also of no avail. Later, he went to Beijing from Xunyang to report everything to Minister Song and asked for relief. Minister Song agreed to issue tens of thousands of yuan in public bonds, but later abandoned the idea because the province's various industries were depressed and there was no way to promote their sale. According to sources in the Finance Department, Finance Director Chen has not yet returned to the province, and the provincial government has repeatedly telegraphed him to return to the province immediately to coordinate everything because hundreds of matters are awaiting disbursement. In addition, in order to alleviate the current problem of maintaining food for the military police suppressing the bandits, the provincial government has decided to levy two months' rent in the provincial capital, which is currently being handled by the Finance Department in conjunction with the municipal finance bureau, with a deadline of half a month to collect it all in order to avoid delaying military operations. As for the financial treasury bonds and interest-bearing short-term circulating bonds issued by the Finance Department, several issues have not been redeemed, and their prices are inevitably declining. The circulating bonds have slightly rebounded because the Finance Department has allocated 300,000 yuan in rice export permits as a redemption fund for May, June, and July. In recent days, they can be used at a 90% rate.

Education is closely related to finance. If funds are exhausted, education cannot develop peacefully. It is found that there are 33 specialized secondary schools and vocational schools in the province, with annual education expenses of about 2 million yuan (salt revenue surcharges are allocated to education and treasury bond funds). These schools have relied on salt revenue surcharges for funding. However, these funds have now been diverted to suppressing the bandits. The previous year's education expenses are in arrears for two months, and this year's (the 19th year) budget has not yet been announced, and there are no funds at all. All public secondary schools and above have not enrolled students and have completely suspended classes. Initially, Director Jiang intended to borrow 500,000 yuan in rice export permits from the Finance Department, with 200,000 yuan for start-up expenses and 300,000 yuan for maintenance expenses. Except for the secondary schools in bandit areas such as Xiushui, Guixi, and Ningdu, which could not open, all the others would open. However, in reality, only tens of thousands of yuan were borrowed. Overseas students had to be remitted quickly because international reputation was at stake, and municipal small subsidies, which were few in number, had to be issued in advance. After paying the above two items, secondary schools and above received one-third of one month's funding, which could only be used for maintenance expenses, and there was no question of opening classes. The municipal primary schools in Nanchang receive only a little over ten thousand yuan per month. Because the municipal government is extremely poor, half a month's salary was owed in the previous year, and there is no funding for this school year. Each primary school receives only a few hundred yuan, and most teachers' salaries are meager, so they cannot be in arrears for long. Therefore, all the teachers and staff of the municipal primary schools unanimously decided not to attend classes until they receive funding. The primary schools that have been open for half a month are still inactive. In addition, only one-third of the compulsory education in each county that is not a bandit county can be taught safely. The entire province's education is almost completely suspended, with tens of thousands of students out of school and thousands of unemployed teachers and staff. It is unknown how the authorities will deal with the aftermath. (September 9th and 11th)

Guangzhou Restaurant Industry Strike 62

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangzhou restaurant and teahouse industry went on strike because they opposed the banquet donation company's use of two-part numbered forms for donation extraction. Those on strike for the 6th and 7th included Nanyuan, Wenyuan, Xiyuan, Dasanyuan, Moshan, Luyu Residence, Chaxiang Room, Yupolou, Yulaochun, Taoliyuan, Yijing, Jupo, Shuangying, and Yutangchun. Western restaurants included Taipingguan, Taiping Branch, Anleyuan, America, and Washington. In addition, there were a total of more than 120 small restaurants and drinking shops. The few that did not strike included Yongchun, Qunle, Jinghua, and Yanchuntai in Chentang, which offer floral entertainment, and a few low-level restaurants. Fearing that the trend would expand and become even more difficult to manage, the Finance Department planned to summon the banquet donation merchants and restaurant industry representatives to the department on the afternoon of the 7th to discuss a solution. However, the restaurant industry did not send representatives to attend, and no solution could be found. Later that night, Chen Fuchou, the owner of Wenyuan, Lin Ji, the owner of Dasanyuan, and Ye Shaopeng, the owner of Moshan, met with the representatives of the donation merchants at the Yongchun Restaurant in Chentang to discuss final mediation methods. Around 10:00 PM, as the meeting was about to end, several police officers arrived at the Yongchun Restaurant and summoned Chen Fuchou, Lin Ji, and Ye Shaopeng to the Chentang Sub-bureau, where they were detained and transferred to the Finance Department's Special Task Force headquarters for custody. It is reported that after the authorities took the three into custody, they planned to first order the major restaurants such as Wenyuan, Nanyuan, Dasanyuan, Xiyuan, and Moshan to resume business as usual before listening to solutions to avoid the trend from expanding. However, the restaurant industry had jointly stamped and resolved to act unanimously before the strike, so their attitude remained unchanged. Furthermore, due to the arrest of Chen, Lin, and Ye, a secret meeting was convened again on the 8th to decide on countermeasures: (1) To insist on the strike until the goal of cancellation is achieved; (2) To issue a declaration requesting criticism from all sectors; (3) To send letters to all related industries for their strong support; (4) To restrict the remaining ten or so restaurants that have not struck to strike together to show their determination. On one hand, each restaurant and shop sent two or three representatives, totaling several hundred people, to the provincial government to petition for the immediate release of the three arrested. Since the restaurant industry's strike, many industries have been affected and goods have been stagnant. In particular, goods that rely on restaurant industry sales and cannot be stored for too long, such as livestock, have been most affected. The market price has therefore tended to fall, so merchants trading with the restaurant industry all hope for an early solution and resumption of business to avoid being affected. However, the Finance Department insists that the implementation of the two-part form is necessary to prevent the concealment of donations and is still insisting on it. (September 8th)

Graduation Ceremony at the Northeastern Military Academy 63

Shenyang Dispatch: The Northeastern Military Academy is the main institution for military education in the Northeast. The graduates have reached the tenth class. The graduates of the previous nine classes have been distributed to the various troops in the Northeast and have become the backbone. Now the tenth class is also graduating. Because Zhang Xueliang was delayed in Huludao and had not returned, it was postponed until the 9th of this month before it was held. This time there are more than 1,700 graduates, divided into 17 teams, including 12 infantry teams, 1 cavalry team, and 2 artillery and engineering teams each. On that day, Zhang Xueliang and other dignitaries all attended. When Zhang arrived at the school, he was wearing a domestically produced gray cloth military uniform. He first went to the reception room for a short rest, and then summoned the 80 students transferred by the Central Government and the 20 students transferred by Liu Chunrong to give separate talks. Then he went to the field to issue certificates and hold the awards ceremony. The awards were divided into first, second, and third class, with ten people in the first class receiving a military knife and a leather clip, ten people in the second class receiving a knife handle case, and ten people in the third class receiving a military knife, all of which were personally awarded by Zhang. Afterwards, he gave a speech to all the students, urging them to always keep the country in mind and never forget their ambitions while at school. After Zhang finished speaking, Yuan Jinkai, the deputy chairman of the Northeastern Political Affairs Committee, and Shi Yixian, the chairman of Liaoning Province, gave speeches, all with the intention of encouraging them. Then, Zhou Lian, the director of education of the Military Academy, gave a reply on behalf of the school. Finally, all the students shouted the oath: "Loyally obey superiors, strive to do my best in battle and defense, do not covet unjust wealth, do not avoid danger within my duty, be determined to defend against insults and protect the people, and swear to wash away all national humiliation." The above six oaths will be faithfully followed throughout my life. After the oath, photos were taken and the meeting adjourned. (September 10th)

Establishment of a 3 Million Loan for the Chinese Eastern Railway 64

Half from the Far Eastern Bank and Half from the Bank of China

The Board of Directors Resolves to Implement Austerity Measures

Harbin Dispatch: The Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) plans to borrow money from banks due to insufficient funds. It is reported that this matter was first negotiated with the British-owned Citibank, and an agreement was largely reached. However, due to jealousy from the Japanese banking community, rumors were fabricated that Russia was transferring the CER to the United States, causing the Russian side to suspend negotiations. However, the railway urgently needs funds and cannot overcome the difficulties without borrowing a large sum of money. Therefore, it has changed to negotiating with the Soviet Russian Far Eastern Bank and our Chinese Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Northeast Three Provinces Bank, and Frontier Bank, and the board of directors has ordered the railway bureau to send the Director of the Funding Department and the Director of the General Accounting Department to be responsible for negotiations. Recently, an agreement has been reached to borrow a total of 3 million yuan, with the Chinese and Russian banks each providing half. The funds can be withdrawn within this week. The interest rate of the Far Eastern Bank is 5%, and the interest rate of the China Bank is 1.2%, with a term of three months. The debt will be repaid after the winter when transportation is prosperous. At the beginning of this month, the railway bureau's revenue and expenditure department and the funds deposited in the bank were only 832,739 yuan, while the accumulated bills to be paid amounted to 2.3 million yuan, including the purchase of materials and the severance pay and pensions due to the laid-off employees. The existing funds are insufficient to pay off the debts, with a shortfall of about 1.5 million rubles. In addition, it is almost the 20th of this month, the day to pay salaries, which requires another 1.5 million rubles. The funds borrowed this time are still insufficient to pay for everything, so it may continue to negotiate loans with other banks. The railway's poor performance this year is mainly due to the impact of the high value of gold and the low value of silver. Green and North Manchurian specialties have always been shipped to Europe in large quantities, and the CER relies on the income from freight to maintain the economy of the entire railway. After the gold rush occurred, European merchants believed that the prices of North Manchurian products, including freight, were higher than those of local European products, so they all stopped purchasing them, causing the specialties to be unable to be shipped out, indirectly causing significant losses to the CER. Although winter specialties can be put on the market, it is feared that the railway's income is still uncertain.

Because the CER is suffering from a shortage of funds, it convened a board of directors meeting on the 8th and resolved to implement austerity measures. The entire plan resolved is as follows: (1) The olive oil refinery and hemp factory will be merged into the General Factory according to the railway bureau's original proposal. (2) The mixed custody of soybeans will be merged into the Commercial Affairs Office. Because the freight solicitation department has been cancelled, it will also be merged into the Commercial Affairs Office. (3) The Hailar wool washing factory has been investigated and found to have no losses and still has annual surpluses. According to the railway bureau's original proposal, it can be placed under the control of the Commercial Affairs Office. (4) It has now been decided to cancel 14 commercial affairs offices along the line from August 15th of this year. The expenses of the provincial offices will be strictly reviewed by the budget committee. (5) The Observatory has already been cancelled, and there are no problems. (6) It is resolved that the Central Library will be changed to the Chinese Eastern Railway Library and will be located in the former Director-General's Office, without adding additional housing. The number of expenses is determined to be over 60,000 yuan in total by both sides. The number of office staff will be divided equally between the two parties. (7) The Water and Electricity Plant will be handled according to the railway bureau's original proposal. (8) The Central Factory of the Works Department will be handled according to the original proposal. The Railway Printing Office can be appropriately increased in funding. (9) The Photography Studio of the Works Department can be handled according to the original proposal. (10) The Tree Cultivation Garden will be handled according to the railway bureau's original proposal, and its budget is determined to be paid half. (11) The Real Estate Department will not be cancelled for the time being, and its budget is determined to be strictly reviewed by the budget committee. (12) A separate budget will be made for the Grand Hotel to ensure that revenue and expenditure are balanced. The railway bureau will not subsidize it, and the hotel staff will not be considered railway staff and will cease all benefits. (13) The soda factory will continue to operate because it is not losing money. (14) According to the Director's report, the sawmill still needs to saw railroad ties and other materials until the end of this year, so it is inconvenient to stop operating for the time being, but its expenses can be reduced. At the same time, the Shitouhezi Sawmill will be closed, and a separate budget will be made from next year. (15) Because the Sino-Russian Vocational School is jointly owned by both parties and is specifically designed to train mid-level technical railway staff, it is inconvenient to transfer it to the Education Department. The budget committee will strictly review the budget, but one more Chinese vice-principal should be added. (16) The Agriculture Section will not be transferred to the Commercial Affairs Office for the time being. This section should be resolved at the same time as the reorganization of the Land Survey Department. All the creamery, pig farm, and horse farm belonging to the section will be cancelled. (17) Part of the Veterinary Department will be cancelled, and the remaining part will be merged into the Medical Department, saving 200,000 yuan per year. (18) The railway bureau should find a way to rent out the Climate Sanatorium for the year. (19) The garage can be rented to private individuals or the expenses can be reduced. (20) The budget of the Editorial Department will be reduced. (21) The Sino-Russian Language Training Institute will remain the same. (22) The Zhalainuoer Coal Mine will first operate on a small scale and explore other coal seams. (23) The Central Printing Office will continue to print tickets as usual. The staff of the office will be divided into two parts. Those who print tickets will be railway staff, and the rest will be hired by the director as business and will not be treated as railway staff. (September 9th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 65

Recruiting a Supplement Camp for Smuggling Suppression to Be Transferred to Songjiang for Training: The supplement recruitment for the 13th and 14th Regiments of the Ministry of Finance's Special Smuggling Suppression Corps has been completed and is awaiting training. Yesterday, the two regiments sent personnel to Songjiang to search for housing and will soon be stationed there for training.

County Government Inquires About Bandits: Pan Yongqiang, the director of the Tinglin Public Security First Branch Bureau, previously captured two bandits, Zhang Abing and Zhu Deru, involved in the robbery of six silver dollars belonging to Zhu Jinhuo. The bandits confessed that the firearms used in the robbery were borrowed from Zhang Ze and Zhu Ruichu, according to the leader. The police were immediately dispatched to Zhang Ze, along with Patrol Officer Yin Zujun, to arrest them. Two pistols and a large bag of colored clothing were found in their home. On the 6th, they were escorted to the county's Public Security Bureau. It is reported that yesterday, County Magistrate Jin sent Mr. Du to conduct the inquiry. According to Zhang Abing's confession, he worked in a tobacco shop in Zhang Ze. During the robbery of Zhu Jinhuo's house last month, he was invited to participate by the leader, and there were nine people in total. They carried muskets, knives, and iron rulers, which were all borrowed from Zhu Ruichu. More than 500 yuan in silver dollars were unearthed under the oxcart shed. The gold, pearls, and banknotes robbed were all taken by the two leaders, and each of us received 56 yuan, he admitted without reservation. Zhu Deru confessed that he was a clerk in Zhu's grocery store, and the rest of his confession was the same. However, according to Zhu Ruichu's confession, the pistol was left in his care by a former bureau director, and he denied providing it to the bandits. However, the interrogating official observed that the pistol was unusually smooth, indicating that it was frequently used, unlike an item left by someone else for storage. He smiled and said nothing about how many members of the Qinggang gang he had taken in. The two bandits Zhang and Zhu were fingerprinted and detained for further interrogation and handling.

Jiashan 66

Gu Lingyun, a Harborer of Bandits, is Arrested: The Jiahu Bandit Suppression Headquarters learned that Gu Lingyun, a farmer in the Yuntian'an area of Xitang Township in the county, was harboring bandits and dividing the spoils. They immediately dispatched a team to the countryside to arrest him and confiscated several pieces of important evidence, which were all escorted to the headquarters for interrogation. In addition, two bandit criminals arrested near Tang were also resolved after interrogation.

Wuxi 67

Wuxi Newspaper Published: Pu Shuying, Shen Yishang, and others in the county raised funds to establish the Wuxi Newspaper, which is scheduled to be published today (15th), one large sheet per day.

Confiscated Inferior Silkworm Eggs to Be Burned on a Scheduled Date: Yi Tingjian, the director of the Sericulture Suppression Office of the Agricultural and Mining Department stationed in Wuxi, recently stated that the number of privately sold and manufactured improved silkworm eggs confiscated in the past, as well as those extracted from various seed farms whose toxicity rate exceeded the prescribed limit, was very large, totaling 18,942 sheets. They should be burned in public on a scheduled date to show the seriousness of the matter. Therefore, it is specifically scheduled to be burned in public at the public sports ground outside the West Gate at 10:00 AM on the 25th of this month.

Changzhou 68

Cheng County Secretly Requests Arrest of Reactionary Criminals: Cai Rushan, a reactionary criminal from Jiangyin, secretly fled to Changzhou and hid in the Xieshengyu Pickled Egg Workshop outside Guanghua Bridge, Xiaonanmen, under the name Fang Zhishou. Li Zonggang, the director of the Jiangyin County Public Security Bureau, learned of this and secretly sent a letter to Tang Renjie, the director of the Wuyi Public Security First Branch Bureau, instructing the police to investigate and arrest him. At the same time, the Jiangyin County Government secretly sent a letter to the Wuyi Public Security Bureau requesting that a team be sent to the Provincial Changzhou High School at Yumeiqiao to arrest Jiang Rongsheng, a student from Jiangyin. The Public Security Bureau and the First Branch Bureau immediately took measures to arrest the two criminals separately and detained Cai Rushan in the local jail and Jiang Rongsheng in the Mukeshell Team headquarters. On the 12th, Li Zonggang, the director of the Jiangyin Public Security Bureau, led the police to Changzhou to pick them up. On the morning of the 13th, the two criminals were taken out, shackled, and escorted back to Cheng County for interrogation.

The Wudan Joint Defense Association Arrests a Known Bandit: The Wudan Joint Defense Association recently learned that the known bandit Ji Gaoshan was hiding on a sand transport ship in the river. The association led the police teams from Benniu and Xiaoche overnight to search and suppress him, and Ji Gaoshan was arrested on the spot, along with seven suspects, who were all escorted to the Xiaochezhen Public Security Third Branch Bureau for interrogation. The suspects were released on bail by the locals, and the bandit leader Ji Gaoshan was escorted to the county on the 14th for interrogation.

A Train Derails in Shidingyan: At around 6:00 PM on the 13th, a troop train departing from Shanghai arrived at Shidingyan, Wuyi County, carrying more than 300 wounded soldiers escorted by Lai Ming, the battalion commander of the First Battalion of the 30th Regiment of the 14th Brigade of the Third Division. For some unknown reason, when traveling to the 164-kilometer mark of the town, one of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo trains suddenly derailed, and the soldiers in the car jumped out in panic, resulting in one death and two seriously injured. After the derailment was dealt with, the train was still driven to Changzhou, and the injured were sent to Wujin Hospital for treatment.

Pinghu 69

Known Bandit Wang Ada Arrested: Yang Cheqing, the captain of the patrol team stationed in Xincang, received a secret report on the 13th stating that bandits had recently been hiding in places such as the Qijiantou area of Luwanmiao and were engaging in large-scale activities. After receiving the report, Captain Yang secretly assembled a plainclothes team of 20 people and set off in two directions at 9:00 AM, one towards Yaqian and one towards Luwanmiao. Captain Yang himself led 20 people to ambush in the Qijiantou area for reinforcement. When the bandits saw the police arrive, they opened fire. The patrol team met the attack head-on and returned fire for about 20 minutes, surrounding a part of the bandit den and arresting Wang Ada, the brother of the known bandit Zhu Luo'amei, on the spot, and seized a six-inch Browning pistol and 17 bullets. According to the bandit's confession, one member of the bandit group was killed and two were injured. The bandits in the Yaqian area had already fled upon hearing the news. After leading the bandit back to Xincang, the captain was ordered by the county magistrate to return to Pinghu in full force. On the afternoon of the 13th, the bandit was escorted to Pinghu and immediately sent to the county government for handling according to the law.

Huzhou 70

Two Steamships on the Changsi Line Robbed: On the night of the 10th of this month, two steamships on the Changsi line, one traveling from Changxing to Sian and one traveling from Sian to Changxing, were docking near Guanyin Bridge when more than a dozen bandits, each armed with a wooden shell pistol and carrying a flashlight, ambushed in the area and fired several shots, ordering them to stop. The bandits then searched both ships at will, and no passengers were spared. It is reported that a large amount of silver dollars and valuables were robbed, and the matter has been reported to the authorities for investigation.

鎭江 71

Measures for Releasing Funds from Cigarette Bond Coupons: The Finance Department yesterday sent a telegram on behalf of the various county governments, stating approximately: "Upon investigation, the issuance of cigarette bond coupons from the nineteenth year has been approved by the Ministry to cease. The funds already collected should be transferred in accordance with Article 2 of the New Bond Coupon Collection Measures, and uniformly used as short-term treasury bonds for customs duties. It is urgently telegraphed that your county magistrate should comply and handle accordingly. If any funds from the nineteenth-year cigarette bond coupons have already been collected, a letter should be sent immediately stating that for those who pay the funds within August, after deducting the 98% discount and 1% handling fee, 97 yuan per hundred yuan should be remitted to the treasury. For those who pay the funds within September, an additional deduction of 1 yuan for the first installment of principal should be made, and 96 yuan per hundred yuan should be remitted to the treasury. All underpaid amounts should be supplemented immediately to clear the account."

Aftermath of Bandit Robbery in Southern Township: The village of Xia Hui in the southern township of Zhenjiang was recently burned and robbed by bandits, resulting in significant damage. According to investigations, a total of 150 households in the village were affected, with 67 households, totaling 142 rooms, burned down. Additionally, Chen Changming, the brother-in-law of He Yunzhong, was burned to death, along with seven oxen and fifty-three fat pigs. Before leaving, the bandits allegedly demanded that He Yanggui pay 8,000 yuan, and He Xiufan and He Xiurong each pay 1,000 yuan and hand over three rifles within ten days.

揚州 72

Another Record of the Copper Coin Interception Case: As reported yesterday, the First Public Security Bureau intercepted a large shipment of privately transported copper coins outside the Quekou city gate. Currently, the copper coins are still stored in the bureau, and the three guards accompanying the shipment, Zhang, Wu, and others, remain detained. Although Shen Runzhi, the owner of the Runchang Qianzhuang (money shop) that shipped the goods, has been making various efforts to seek a solution, he has not made significant progress. The Chamber of Commerce has twice requested the county government to leniently release the individuals based on the situation, but the county government has yet to respond. However, the number of copper coins reported by the bureau is ten cartloads, while rumors and local newspapers claim there were twenty cartloads. This discrepancy has attracted attention from various parties, and the county government is taking the matter very seriously.

南通 73

Jiangbei Communist Bandits Split and Kill Each Other: Communist Party members in the Jiangbei counties of Tongtai collude with local bandits to create disturbances and cause great harm. Recently, many bandits have surrendered to government troops and pledged allegiance, with over 800 having been granted rehabilitation. These bandits have declared their unwillingness to be exploited by the Communist Party any further. Internal conflict and killings between communist bandits are occurring in areas bordering Tai. Li Mingyang, the director of the Provincial Security Department, is currently supervising the Security Regiment in suppressing them.

County Police Officer Dies in Gun Test: Li Hanbin, the deputy captain of the county police force, obtained a hand-held machine gun while suppressing bandits in Erluan. He accidentally shot himself in the abdomen while testing it, and died at 9:00 PM on the 12th.

Joint Defense in the Northwest Fourth District: Due to the rampant activity of communist bandits and the repeated devastation of the northwest districts of the county, the county government, in light of the recent looting of the town of Wujieqiao in Pingchao by communist bandits, resulting in the complete destruction of the town, an emergency meeting was convened by various sectors, which decided that the four districts of Pingchao, Baipu, Tangzha, and Liuqiao in the northwest would immediately implement a joint defense.

高郵 74

Anhui Bandits Intend to Invade Youjing: The notorious bandit Jiang Guochang of Anhui Province recently led 500-600 bandits to besiege Tongcheng Town, under the jurisdiction of Tianchang County. It is reported that Jiang's bandits were fiercely resisted by the garrison troops and the self-defense corps of Tongcheng Town, and reinforcements from Tianchang County arrived, so they were unable to succeed. They looted the nearby villages, occupied Xiaoyun Mountain, and ordered the bandit leader Wang Qitaiye to lead his men to attack Licheng Town, under the jurisdiction of Bao'ying County. Fortunately, the gun towers in the town were able to resist, repelling the bandits. On the afternoon of the 10th, they attacked again, but Bao'ying County had dispatched naval and land police teams to the town for reinforcement, making it difficult for the bandits to achieve their goal. It is now reported that they intend to invade towns such as Yingjiaqiao and Jingou in Gaoyou County, causing panic among the people. Wealthy households are moving away, and the town chiefs have jointly petitioned the county government to send troops quickly to strengthen defenses and deter the bandits.

Detailed Report on the Drowning of the Woman with the Surname Xue: Xue Jixing, a farmer from the sixth village of the second district of the county, married Chen Yuedian, the daughter of Yang Hanxiang, last year. Chen had been suffering from an external illness, so she stayed at her mother's house to seek medical treatment. She gradually recovered and returned home alone on the 30th of last month. However, she accidentally fell into the river west of Xiaolizhuang and drowned. Chen Yuedian heard the news the next day and confirmed that it was her daughter. She then hired laborers, along with relatives Chen Shaoxuan and Chen Guoming, to carry the body to Xue Jixing's house. They used iron chains to lock Jixing's wife to the corpse. After much mediation, Xue Jixing was persuaded to pay 400 yuan for funeral expenses. Xue had agreed, but the village chief Chen Shaoxuan intervened. Xue then appealed to the county government for an autopsy. The county government dispatched Zhou Shaoji with a coroner to conduct the autopsy. The village chief Chen Shaoxuan led over 100 people to disrupt the scene. Zhou Shaoji repeatedly tried to pacify them before they dispersed. The autopsy confirmed that the cause of death was drowning. The trial was held yesterday. After the interrogation, both parties were instructed to post bail and await investigation. However, village chief Chen Shaoxuan is suspected of attempted extortion and has been detained for further investigation.

杭州 75

Reorganization of County Defense Corps: The Provincial Government's Security Department has established a fifth section to reorganize the defense corps in all counties of Zhejiang Province, with an office established on Wushan Road. Detailed plans are in place for improving all aspects of the provincial defense corps. As for the training of the county defense corps, it has been decided that the department will send personnel to train them separately, with a set timeframe to cultivate elite troops to protect the area. The training personnel will be selected by this section, and the announcement should be made soon.

Telephone Bureau Uses Female Switchboard Operators: The Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau, to improve telephone connections, has decided to use female operators for all branch bureaus. This is because women are gentle and quiet, making them suitable for switchboard operation. Yesterday, Jiao Xiu, Yang Aizhen, and two others were assigned as long-distance switchboard operators for the Lanxi City branch bureau. Shen Minying and others were assigned as long-distance operators for the Jiaxing branch bureau. In addition, branch bureaus in counties such as Yin, Shaoxing, and Yongjia will also be assigning three female operators in the coming days.

寗波 76

Bandits Disarm Police Station at Buliangqiao: At 7:00 PM on the 10th, many bandits suddenly broke into the Buliangqiao Police Station in Yinnan, claiming to disarm the police. The police were few in number and dared not resist, so the bandits took away all their firearms. At that time, a woman surnamed Yang, who lived nearby, heard the noise and went outside to watch. The bandits fired a shot to warn her, and she ran into the alley. The bandits fired another shot and fled. The woman died of fright and her husband, Yang Ayou, reported the incident to the court, which sent someone to investigate.

Fire at Sanjiaodi: At about 12:00 AM last night (the 12th), a fire broke out accidentally at the Wantai Rice Shop in Sanjiaodi in this city. It took about an hour to extinguish. More than ten houses of neighboring businesses, including a cake shop, a silk thread shop, and a soy milk shop on the front street, were burned down, resulting in a loss of several thousand gold.

上虞 77

Civil Affairs Department Approves the County Boundary of Lihaisuo: Lihaisuo borders the two counties of Shangyu and Shaoxing. In April, the Civil Affairs Department commissioned instructor Shi Fuchang to work with the two county magistrates to jointly delineate the complex county boundary at Lihaisuo. The department has now approved the demarcation based on Shi’s report, using the intersection of the crossroads in Lihaisuo as the boundary line, with the southwest gates within the city under the jurisdiction of Shangyu, and the northeast gates under the jurisdiction of Shaoxing. Other areas will remain unchanged for the time being. Both county governments are required to clearly hand over the residents, household registration, land registers, and other documents immediately. The Shaoxing government has already consulted with this county government to schedule the handover procedures.

Two Prisoners Escape: Xu Guixiang, sentenced to six months imprisonment for a smoking case, and two criminals being escorted from Yuyao, who pretended to be military officers, escaped from their cages at around 3:00 AM on the night of the 9th during a heavy snowstorm, by destroying the thick walls. Chen Tingnan, the prison guard, has reported the escape to the county for investigation and arrest.

News on the Defense of Lihaisuo: Lihaisuo is located near the rear sea, and piracy has been rampant recently, with frequent kidnappings, causing panic among the people. Recently, Yang Yuechuan, a village committee member, has consulted with the governments of Shangyu and Shaoxing counties, requesting them to send security teams to station there permanently. It is reported that the two county governments have agreed, and Yang has also invited local gentry to add to the local defense corps, so that they can work together with the security teams to maintain local security.

Lu Province Schools Have Difficulty Opening 78

| Affected by Military Affairs |

May Open on October 1st

Jinan Correspondence: Due to the impact of the war, secondary and higher schools in the province have not yet opened. It is heartbreaking that 12 provincial middle schools, 4 normal schools, 2 rural normal schools, 1 senior high school, 1 women's normal school, 2 vocational schools, 1 women's vocational school, and 1 women's middle school, with a total of five or six thousand young students, have been interrupted in their studies. Students from wealthier families have mostly gone to other provinces to enroll in classes, while poorer students are unable to do so and can only lament their helplessness. Private schools that could not recruit students in previous years are now overcrowded, with most of the students having transferred from provincial schools. However, there are more students than schools can accommodate, with only less than 5% being accepted. The Education Department has repeatedly convened meetings of the principals of these schools to discuss solutions, but it is difficult for even the cleverest housewife to cook without rice. He Siyuan, the director of the Education Department, has been discussing with the newly appointed Chairman Han Fuju, and they have decided to reduce the scope and simplify matters to barely open the schools. The plan is to temporarily exclude schools north of the Yellow River, and to reduce the budget of the remaining provincial schools by half, merging classes to save money and barely open the schools. It is rumored that the schools may open on October 1st.

Cai Yuanpei and Dai Jitao Resign as University Presidents 79

The presidents of national universities are mostly important figures in the Party and the state, holding multiple positions, which makes it difficult for them to focus on education. Jiang Menglin, the Minister of Education, recognizing this, resigned as president of Zhejiang University. Dai Jitao, the president of the Examination Yuan, who also served as president of Sun Yat-sen University, and Cai Yuanpei, the president of the Academia Sinica, who also served as president of Peking University, have also recently submitted their resignations to the Ministry of Education, which were then forwarded to the National Government for approval. It is believed that university presidents must devote themselves wholeheartedly to education. Zhu Jiahua and Chen Daqi have been recommended to take over their respective positions. The Ministry of Education has already forwarded Dai's resignation to the National Government, which has been approved at a meeting. It is rumored that Cai's resignation may be approved at the next National Government meeting.

Local News

Shanghai Students Who Pass Qualification Review Should Pay Attention 81

Can Transfer to the Last Grade to Study

The Ministry of Education ordered all directly administered universities and provincial and municipal education departments to allow students from private vocational schools and above that have not been registered or have been closed down after qualification review to transfer to the last grade to study. The order of the Education Department is recorded as follows:

According to the investigation, students from private vocational schools and above that have not been registered or have been closed down in Shanghai who have passed the qualification review have been notified by the Ministry to be admitted to public and registered private vocational schools and above. However, according to Article 7 of the Qualification Examination Regulations for Graduates and Students of Private Vocational Schools and Above in Beijing and Shanghai that have not been Registered or have been Closed Down, students with excellent grades may transfer to the last grade of public or registered private vocational schools and above during the admission process (this is the result of the qualification examination, and the Ministry of Education orders public and registered private vocational schools and above to be lenient and not restricted by Article 4 of the University Regulations and Article 4 of the Vocational School Regulations). Other graduates and students should transfer to the corresponding grades according to their level. All schools should comply with this order. In addition to separate orders, this order is also issued to the relevant departments for investigation and notification.

Sports

China and England Obtain the Right to the Robert Cup Final 86

China Defeats the United States 6-4, 6-4, 6-2

England Defeats Portugal 8-6, 6-4, 6-2

China and England Win the Right to the Robert Cup Final in Shanghai. In the semi-finals at the French Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon, China defeated the tenacious United States 6-4, 6-4, 6-2, and England defeated Portugal 8-6, 6-4, 6-2. The details of the two matches are recorded below.

(1) The Brilliant Match Between Lin Qiu and the United States 87

The match between China and the United States began at 3:00 PM. Both sides put on a brilliant performance, and the competition was fierce. The Chinese representatives, Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai, fought hard and dared not relax. The US representatives, Squier and Bode, also fought bravely and refused to be outdone. The interest in the match overflowed to the more than 200 spectators, who were moved by every word and action. It can be said that this was the most intense and brilliant doubles match in the current Robert Cup.

Mr. Squier of the US team is lean and strong, enduring and tireless. His shots and serves are powerful, but he lacks control. As for his net play, he has already mastered two-thirds of it. He imitated Lin Baohua's feinting tactics, and with a light flick of the ball at the net, the ball shot out sideways, leaving Lin Qiu of China helpless. He was greatly praised by the audience. Bode was a former strong player, with powerful serves and good net play, but he lost many points overall. In short, the two men's skills were very different from the Rotary Cup matches, with a world of difference. If there were no Lin Qiu of China in the championship, they would have easily swept Shanghai and won the championship. Even the British and Portuguese players, who are the heroes of the time, would have been intimidated. What a pity for the United States.

Observing the performance of Lin Qiu of China, it has reached the peak. Qiu Feihai's catch was greatly praised, but he lost more points yesterday, which was a shortcoming. Mr. Lin Baohua was the most energetic of the four. The two Americans were very afraid of his cannonball serve, and few could return it. Therefore, Lin's serve scored at least twenty points yesterday, which was truly amazing. Usually, Lin's first serve is very heavy, but if it doesn't go over the net, the power of the second serve is reduced. But yesterday it was different, the power of the two serves was average, without distinguishing between light and heavy, so it was especially admired by the audience. His forehand shot also had a grip, which can be said to be his masterpiece. The two men's connection was very tight, and their net skills were impeccable. Both sides fought with all their strength, and the ball was extremely sharp. Everyone showed their best skills. Lin Qiu's victory was fortunate, but the defeat of the US military was also admirable.

First Set: Bode's serve was accurate and fast, and he won the first game. When Lin Baohua served, the United States fought hard with a downward momentum, and the fight was fierce. Lin Qiu cautiously fought and managed to win two games in a row. The US military was unwilling to be weak and fought hard to pull back a game. Then each won a game, and the score was tied at three games each. The competition was even fiercer, and no one was willing to relax. The battle dragged on and was difficult to separate. Lin Qiu won two games in a row with ingenuity, and then Bode served and won four chips, becoming 5-4. Lin Baohua returned the color with a heavy ball, and as a result, Lin Qiu won the first set 6-4.

Second Set: At the beginning of the second set, both sides continued to fight, and the situation was tense. The US military took the lead many times, and Lin Qiu followed behind. After 3-3, Lin Qiu took the lead in one leap, but they had used up all their energy to overtake by 5-3. There were many styles on both sides, and the audience applauded and cheered. Although the US military regained a game, Lin Qiu won again 6-4.

Third Set: At the beginning of the third set, Lin Qiu showed off their smashing skills, and the ball was well-proportioned, accurate, and fast. The US military also had a wonderful way to respond by intercepting at the net. The ball went back and forth on the net like electricity, and the audience's vision was disturbed. Unconsciously, the cheers suddenly made the atmosphere on the field even more tense. The US military fought hard and won the first game, but after this, Lin Qiu's brilliance became more and more intense. Although the US military continued to fight hard, they finally had no way to do anything. Lin Qiu made a downward momentum, and in an instant, they won five games in a row. It was not easy to win all five games so easily. It can be seen from this that Lin Qiu's skills are very good. After each winning a game, Lin Qiu returned in triumph with a score of 6-2.

(2) England Wins the Fierce Battle Against Portugal 88

After the Sino-US war, the bell rang four times, and the British and Portuguese players took the stage to fight. The British players were Hughes and Stock, and the Portuguese players were Canavaro and Korasa. In the second set, England took a 5-1 lead and had a great momentum, but Canavaro of Portugal fought hard, and the two British players showed their skills in a majestic manner, adding five games in a row and climbing to the top with 6-5. But after that, the British military tried to attack Korasa of Portugal, and Korasa had difficulty parrying, resulting in failure. England won with a score of 8-6. It was a pity for the defeat of the Portuguese army. In the next two sets, it was easier for the British to win. However, the British players ran back and forth and seemed very tired. As a result, England won the second and third sets with a score of 6-4 and 6-2.

Business News

Finance: Gold Prices Trended Soft Last Week 95

Trading Was Quiet Throughout the Week: Gold prices were slightly weaker last week, with daily fluctuations of about four to five taels. The price hovered around 560 taels, showing a flat trend. This was due to both buyers and sellers controlling the market as the settlement date approached, to prevent sharp fluctuations. Learning from the past experience of the previous settlement, sellers dared not overextend themselves, and buyers were wary of extending bills of exchange. Therefore, both sides remained cautious. However, market sentiment remained anxious, leading to occasional complex situations. A brief overview of the past week is provided below:

Full Week Down 6.1 Taels: On Monday, September 8, both tael silver and silver prices saw a pullback. Bills of exchange remained unchanged, but the internal dynamics of banks seemed to ease. The initial price for October gold opened at 561.7 taels, then dropped by one tael due to the political turmoil in Japan, causing market sentiment to turn downward. Later, the market stabilized around 60 taels, closing at 61.4 taels in the afternoon, still 0.3 taels lower than the previous Saturday. The next day, the silver market recovered and the exchange rate weakened, causing the gold market to soften. However, there were fluctuations of about six taels, reaching 65.5 taels in the afternoon before retreating to 61 taels as Indian exchange rates recovered and bankers aggressively sold orders. Furthermore, Yuan Mao, Yongfeng, and Cuitai actively sold off their holdings. Wednesday saw a flat market with only three taels of fluctuations. Dealers were unwilling to sell actively, and both buyers and sellers were in a wait-and-see mode, creating a stagnant situation. The market initially rose by over one tael to 62.3 taels in the morning, with tael silver remaining unchanged and silver prices slightly higher. However, internal trends in sterling weakened, and the price reached 63.4 taels before slightly reversing in the afternoon. The market closed at 61.8 taels, 0.8 taels higher than the previous day. Dealers such as Chengfeng and Yongchang bought in, while Bianxinshengda sold. On Thursday, the silver market weakened, but the United States seemed to be selling, causing the gold market to rise. However, trading was scarce and the market was very quiet, with only about two taels of price difference. The market closed at 62.7 taels. The following day saw fluctuations in tael silver, but there was no development overseas and the United States had no intention of buying or selling. The gold market suddenly experienced turmoil, with fluctuations of up to ten taels throughout the day. This was due to the panic caused by the political turmoil in Japan, which made the market fearful. The market was initially flat in the morning, but large investors tended to sell off, breaking the 60-tael mark. Bills of exchange weakened significantly, and companies such as Shengshengda sold off their holdings. The market closed at 52.8 taels in the afternoon, a sharp drop of ten taels compared to the previous day. On Saturday, the silver market recovered, and bills of exchange, which had been weakening since the previous Friday by 1.5 levels, had not changed for seven or eight days. It was not until the previous Saturday (13th) that they were raised by one level, while the gold market tended to stabilize. This was due to the divergent trends in sterling and the fact that banks were settling accounts. With the settlement date approaching, Zhifeng, Yongda, and others were seeking to buy, and market sentiment turned bullish. The market closed at 56.6 taels, an increase of 3.8 taels, and then rose again by over one tael, with fluctuations of about five taels in half a day. Compared to the previous Saturday (6th), it was still down 6.1 taels. The high and low prices for British, American, Indian silver markets, bills of exchange, and gold prices are listed below:

Yesterday was Sunday, and all Chinese and foreign banks were closed as usual. Sunday Interbank Loan Rates Remain Strong 97

The Broad Angle Has Risen to 6 Qian 3 Fen and a Half

Yesterday was Sunday, and the market was typically quiet. The interbank loan rate was 7 qian 3 fen and 0.02 hao for both morning and afternoon markets, the same as the afternoon market on the previous day. Silver loan rate was 1 fen higher, at 6 fen. The morning and afternoon markets were also identical. The morning market saw a clearing of 245,000 yuan in bills and no market for banknotes. The afternoon market saw a clearing of 326,000 yuan in bills and 10,000 yuan in banknotes. The off-market banknote market was 85,000 yuan in the morning and 30,000 yuan in the afternoon. Money shops collected and settled over 2.1 million yuan in silver public bills and over 27 million yuan in foreign public bills. All types of silver and foreign settlements and transactions with banks were closed and there was no news. Transactions of small money shops amounted to over 300,000 yuan. The market for subsidiary coins remained unchanged for Jiangnan small foreign coins at 6 qian 4 fen 7 li. The morning market was the same, with only 2,000 yuan traded in the morning. However, the Guangdong small foreign coins rose sharply again to 6 qian 3 fen 4 li in the morning market and 6 qian 3 fen 5 li in the afternoon market, an increase of 3 li compared to the previous morning market. Transactions totaled 200,000 yuan in the morning market and 85,000 yuan in the afternoon market. Copper coins increased by 1,000 to 388,000 cash.

Cotton Yarn: Yarn Market Very Sluggish Last Week 99

The yarn market appeared quite uneasy last week, mainly due to the weakness of the global cotton industry and the domestic turmoil caused by widespread warfare and banditry, which severely impacted sales. The stock of unsold goods at various mills continued to increase. According to some sources, it was approximately 150,000 bales. With such a large amount of inventory, it became even more difficult for yarn prices to rise. As a result, the majority of people in the market were bearish. Although the Cantonese traders and certain manufacturers tried their best to purchase, they could not support the market on their own. Therefore, the Cantonese traders had to painfully liquidate their forward contracts, causing even more panic among retail investors. The market had no support, and prices for all months plummeted by over 50 taels. In addition, approximately 160,000-170,000 bales of 20s and 10s Japanese yarn that were previously offered by Japanese mills were mostly accepted by traders and customers who intended to sell them in the autumn. However, due to the poor market environment and the difficulty in selling the yarn, there was a lot of volatility. Therefore, the selling pressure from the Chaozhou traders increased, and the selling price of Japanese yarn continued to decline rapidly. In short, the large inventory, stagnant sales, and unstable political situation were the biggest obstacles to yarn sales. The price of cotton yarn for each month fell by 3 taels compared to the previous week. The total turnover for the week was 114,250 bales. The spot yarn market was even more sluggish. The Sichuan and Tianjin traders bought a lot of futures. The total amount of spot and futures purchased by various traders for the week was 9,761 bales, and the amount of yarn traded among peers was 2,950 bales. Zhabei: Yesterday, only a few boats arrived from inland areas, and river stocks were extremely low. However, the stocks in factory warehouses were better than market sales. Top-quality rice was particularly strong, priced at 20 yuan and 78 jiao. Medium-quality japonica rice was slightly trimmed, and large wholesale orders were slightly better, mainly because both stocks and arrivals were low, and transactions were normal. Dozens of shi of Western new japonica rice continued to arrive, but it was ordinary goods from the Central Plains, so the price was only 19 and a half yuan. Top-quality goods were still priced at 20 yuan. Although there was a source of Eastern new japonica rice from outside the customs, most of it was in the hands of rice mill traders, so very few were sold. The market initially tried to maintain a high price, but buyers were not greedy and the price was flat, similar to the previous day. However, it is feared that the price outside the market will have to go downstream. New sheep-tip rice opened high at 15 yuan, with a slight difference of 1-2 jiao. This type of market seems difficult to stand, and a large batch will arrive later. New guest-tip rice was also weak, down 2-3 jiao, and buying interest waned. Top-quality goods gradually approached 14 yuan, and ordinary goods were all around 13 and a half yuan. Both the arrival and sales of Bian Yuan were weak, and there was still no increase or decrease.

South Shanghai: There were very few arrivals from the river, and the market was flat and weak. Only medium and low-quality broken japonica rice was on the market, and top-quality goods were missing. Therefore, the price barely opened at 19 yuan and 78 jiao. South Traders: The sales of thin rice were limited, and there were very few arrivals. The market price was still hovering around 20 yuan and 89 jiao. There were very few sources of Eastern new japonica rice this time, and the price followed the Northern market. Although new japonica rice arrived in the South, the demand in this street was not smooth, and the price remained the same. Arrivals of sheep-tip new-tip rice were scarce, and the market was flat and weak. White Yuan has been short of arrivals for days. Even if there were a few scattered goods, sales were not strong, so the market was sluggish.
