Shanghai Market

Market News 166

Yu Lun Silk and Embroidery Bureau on the east end of Wangping Street, Nanjing Road, announces that the bureau officially opened on the 1st of this month with a grand discount for thirty days. Recently, sales of autumn clothing have been quite brisk. Prices for various goods, such as new-style patterned and plain broadcloth and flannel, range from 75 cents to 1.45 yuan per foot. The new Qilin crepe produced by the Hangzhou Zhendan Factory is sturdy in quality and novel in design, selling for only about two yuan per foot. Today is Sunday, and we have prepared high-quality silk scarves as gifts for customers to express our preferential treatment and to commemorate the occasion, and so on.

Feng Taichang Foreign Goods Store, located opposite the Little World amusement park inside the New North Gate, announces that the store is organized by Mr. Hu Yizhi. Its purpose is to specialize in domestic famous factory products and also handle miscellaneous goods from European and American countries. The business aims to promote both retail and wholesale sales, especially welcoming customers from near and far. The store has been renovated and is now open for business, with a formal opening to follow soon, and so on.

Hua Tong Food Company announces that it has been in business for eighteen years, making it a leader in the food industry in Shanghai. Its various food products far surpass imported goods and can hold its own among Western products. Its sales are so strong that even orders from the South Seas Islands are overwhelming. Recently, a new type of three-pound, four-color edged tin and five-pound Red Tree brand square container has been released, with a brilliant trademark and exquisite filling. Therefore, the busyness of work is unprecedented in recent years, and so on.

Qunfang Photography Company at the intersection of Guangxi Road and Shantou Road announces that the company is officially opening on September 16th according to the Gregorian calendar. The photographers hired are all art experts, and the scenery is also magnificent. It is said that those who go to take pictures during the opening period can get a 30% discount, and so on.

The Pathé Company at the corner of Renji Road and Sichuan Road announces that due to recent letters from young ladies and talented women in Shanghai and Suzhou requesting the recording of "Pearl Pagoda" storytelling records, the company has spared no expense to invite famous storytellers Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing to record four "Pearl Pagoda" records. One of them is a solo performance by Shen, and the other three are duets by both. In addition, the company felt dissatisfied with the female roles in the previously released "Farewell My Concubine" by Jin Shaoshan and recently re-invited Jin Ling to re-record it with the famous Kun opera actress Xiao Juhong as a partner to achieve a complementary effect. The above five records are scheduled to be released on the first of next month, and so on.

Publishing News 167

The Chinese Women's Temperance Association announces that in order to promote family happiness, improve social evils, reject tobacco, alcohol, gambling, and evil, and advocate kindness, filial piety, chastity, and thrift, in addition to establishing a Women and Children's Education and Care Institute in Jiangwan to actually help beggars, maids, abandoned women, and other groups, it also publishes a monthly temperance publication to spread propaganda. In order to implement the association's advocacy and make the public understand the association's work, the association is now offering a reward for essays, hoping that comrades at home and abroad will generously contribute. The association welcomes such contributions and hereby lists the essay rules: (A) Topics: (1) The future of tobacco prohibition in China; (2) Aspects of charitable work in China that need improvement; (3) How to improve the lives of farmers, workers, and women (Authors can choose one of the above three topics, with a word count of 2,500 to 5,000 words). (B) Prizes: First place, 50 yuan; second place, 30 yuan; third place, 10 yuan. (C) Deadline: The deadline for submissions is the end of December of this year; late submissions will not be accepted. Submission address: Editorial Department, Chinese Women's Temperance Association, No. 23 Yuanmingyuan Road, Shanghai, and so on.

Medical News 168

Dr. Tao Yiqing, residing at No. 38 Tiandeng Street in the South City, is the son of the famous physician Tao Yinkang. He has inherited his family's scholarship and is proficient in medicine. Now that the autumn weather is cool and diseases are rampant, even the family of the educator Jiang Tiqing has been affected, with several members suffering. The youngest son is in the most critical condition, having been unable to eat for seven or eight days. Dr. Tao has been able to cure him and others with his skillful diagnosis and treatment. Therefore, society often says, "With Tao Yiqing, there is no need to fear illness," and so on.

Theater News 169

The Empire Grand Theatre announces that it will be screening the Shanghai social realism film "The Tragedy of the Dancing Girl" starting today. In order to provide excellent entertainment to the audience, the theater has also hired the famous Korean magic troupe from Shanghai to perform on stage day and night, presenting their unique act of "Beautiful Woman Body Switch" and "Shooting the Beauty." Such a famous film and excellent stage performance are rare opportunities, so please do not miss them, and so on.
